<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:122px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Latex_real_numbers_square.svg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="341" data-file-width="343" decoding="async" height="119" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d0/Latex_real_numbers_square.svg/120px-Latex_real_numbers_square.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d0/Latex_real_numbers_square.svg/180px-Latex_real_numbers_square.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d0/Latex_real_numbers_square.svg/240px-Latex_real_numbers_square.svg.png 2x" width="120"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Latex_real_numbers_square.svg" title="放大"></a></div><b>實數</b>集的表示符號 (<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \mathbb {R} }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mi mathvariant="double-struck">R</mi>
</mrow>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \mathbb {R} }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\R" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/786849c765da7a84dbc3cce43e96aad58a5868dc" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.678ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>)</div></div></div>
<p>在<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E6%95%B8%E5%AD%B8" title="數學">數學</a>中，<b>实数</b>是<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E6%9C%89%E7%90%86%E6%95%B8" title="有理數">有理數</a>和<a href="/wiki/%E7%84%A1%E7%90%86%E6%95%B8" title="無理數">無理數</a>的总称，前者如<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle 0}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mn>0</mn>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle 0}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle 0}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/2aae8864a3c1fec9585261791a809ddec1489950" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.162ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>、<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle -4}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">

</mrow>

</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle -4}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/addc8519724f81b43a6883c5eb2c996f9fc2996f" style="vertical-align: -0.505ex; width:2.971ex; height:2.343ex;"/></span>、<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle {\frac {81}{7}}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">

<mn>7</mn>
</mfrac>
</mrow>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle {\frac {81}{7}}}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle {\frac {81}{7}}}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/772fe391e9a16ae2073fa6da4415099488acef71" style="vertical-align: -2.005ex; width:3.161ex; height:5.343ex;"/></span>；后者如<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle {\sqrt {2}}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">

</msqrt>
</mrow>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle {\sqrt {2}}}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\sqrt {2}}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/b4afc1e27d418021bf10898eb44a7f5f315735ff" style="vertical-align: -0.671ex; width:3.098ex; height:3.009ex;"/></span>、<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \pi }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>π<!-- π --></mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \pi }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\pi " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/9be4ba0bb8df3af72e90a0535fabcc17431e540a" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.332ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>等。实数可以<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E7%9B%B4%E8%A7%80" title="直觀">直观</a>地看作<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%B0%8F%E6%95%B8" title="小數">小數</a>（<a href="/wiki/%E6%9C%89%E9%99%90%E5%B0%8F%E6%95%B0" title="有限小数">有限</a>或<a href="/wiki/%E6%97%A0%E9%99%90%E5%B0%8F%E6%95%B0" title="无限小数">無限</a>的），它們能把<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E6%95%B0%E8%BD%B4" title="数轴">数轴</a>「填滿」。但僅僅以<a href="/wiki/%E6%9E%9A%E4%B8%BE" title="枚举">枚舉</a>的方式不能描述實數的全体。实数和<a href="/wiki/%E8%99%9A%E6%95%B0" title="虚数">虚数</a>共同构成<a href="/wiki/%E5%A4%8D%E6%95%B0_(%E6%95%B0%E5%AD%A6)" title="复数 (数学)">复数</a>。
</p><p>根据日常经验，<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E6%9C%89%E7%90%86%E6%95%B8%E9%9B%86" title="有理數集">有理數集</a>在數軸上似乎是「<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E7%A8%A0%E5%AF%86" title="稠密">稠密</a>」的，于是古人一直认为用有理數即能滿足<a class="mw-disambig" href="/wiki/%E6%B8%AC%E9%87%8F" title="測量">測量</a>上的實際需要。以邊長為<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle 1}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mn>1</mn>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle 1}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="1" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/92d98b82a3778f043108d4e20960a9193df57cbf" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.162ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>公分的正方形為例，其對角線有多長？在規定的精度下（比如<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E8%AA%A4%E5%B7%AE" title="誤差">誤差</a>小於<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle 0.001}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mn>0.001</mn>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle 0.001}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle 0.001}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/3361411641bbe8caea51bf59e30f7caf87d0d7cb" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:5.297ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>公分），總可以用有理數來表示足夠精確的測量結果（比如<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle 1.414}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mn>1.414</mn>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle 1.414}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle 1.414}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/60806674f032e76236bfdbd8d69fb325223726a2" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:5.297ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>公分）。但是，<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%8F%A4%E5%B8%8C%E8%87%98" title="古希臘">古希臘</a><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E6%AF%95%E8%BE%BE%E5%93%A5%E6%8B%89%E6%96%AF%E5%AD%A6%E6%B4%BE" title="毕达哥拉斯学派">畢達哥拉斯學派</a>的數學家發現，只使用有理數無法完全<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E7%B2%BE%E7%A2%BA" title="精確">精確</a>地表示這條對角線的長度，這徹底地打擊了他們的數學理念；他們原以為：
</p>
<ul><li>任何兩條線段（的長度）的比，可以用<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E8%87%AA%E7%84%B6%E6%95%B8" title="自然數">自然數</a>的比來表示。</li></ul>
<p>正因如此，<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E7%95%A2%E9%81%94%E5%93%A5%E6%8B%89%E6%96%AF" title="畢達哥拉斯">畢達哥拉斯</a>本人甚至有「萬物皆數」的信念，這裡的數是指自然數（<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle 1,2,3,\ldots }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mn>1</mn>
<mo>,</mo>
<mn>2</mn>
<mo>,</mo>
<mn>3</mn>
<mo>,</mo>
<mo>…<!-- … --></mo>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle 1,2,3,\ldots }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle 1,2,3,\ldots }" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/ee2ad0c84eec6102f704be18a9e709cec4029faf" style="vertical-align: -0.671ex; width:9.312ex; height:2.509ex;"/></span>），而由自然數的比就得到所有正有理數，而有理數集存在「縫隙」這一事實，對當時很多數學家來說可謂極大的打擊；見<a href="/wiki/%E7%AC%AC%E4%B8%80%E6%AC%A1%E6%95%B8%E5%AD%B8%E5%8D%B1%E6%A9%9F" title="第一次數學危機">第一次數學危機</a>。
</p><p>從<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%8F%A4%E5%B8%8C%E8%87%98" title="古希臘">古希臘</a>一直到17世紀，<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E6%95%B8%E5%AD%B8%E5%AE%B6" title="數學家">數學家</a>們才慢慢接受無理數的存在，並把它和有理數平等地看作<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E6%95%B8" title="數">數</a>；後來有<a href="/wiki/%E8%99%9A%E6%95%B0" title="虚数">虚数</a>概念的引入，為加以區別而稱作“實數”，意即“實在的數”。在當時，儘管虛數已經出現並廣為使用，實數的嚴格定義卻仍然是個難題，以至<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%87%BD%E6%95%B8" title="函數">函數</a>、<a href="/wiki/%E6%9E%81%E9%99%90_(%E6%95%B0%E5%AD%A6)" title="极限 (数学)">極限</a>和<a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E6%94%B6%E6%96%82%E6%80%A7&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="收斂性（页面不存在）">收斂性</a>的概念都被定義清楚之後，才由十九世紀末的<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E6%88%B4%E5%BE%B7%E9%87%91" title="戴德金">戴德金</a>、<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%BA%B7%E6%89%98%E5%B0%94" title="康托尔">康托尔</a>等人對實數進行了嚴格處理。
</p><p>所有实数的集合則可稱為<b>实数系</b>（real number system）或<b>实数连续统</b>。任何一个完备的阿基米德有序域均可称为实数系。在保序同构意义下它是惟一的，常用<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \mathbb {R} }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mi mathvariant="double-struck">R</mi>
</mrow>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \mathbb {R} }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\R" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/786849c765da7a84dbc3cce43e96aad58a5868dc" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.678ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>表示。由于<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \mathbb {R} }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mi mathvariant="double-struck">R</mi>
</mrow>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \mathbb {R} }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\R" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/786849c765da7a84dbc3cce43e96aad58a5868dc" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.678ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>是定义了算数运算的运算系统，故有实数系这个名称。<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-1"><a href="#cite_note-1">[1]</a></sup>
</p>

<h2><span id=".E5.88.9D.E7.AD.89.E6.95.B8.E5.AD.B8"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="初等數學">初等數學</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%AE%9E%E6%95%B0&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="编辑章节：初等數學">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>在目前的<a href="/wiki/%E5%88%9D%E7%AD%89%E6%95%B0%E5%AD%A6" title="初等数学">初等數學</a>中，没有對實數進行嚴格的定義，而一般把實數看作<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%B0%8F%E6%95%B8" title="小數">小數</a>（有限或無限的）。实数的完备性可以利用幾何加以说明，即数轴上的點與實數一一對應；見<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E6%95%B0%E8%BD%B4" title="数轴">数轴</a>。
</p><p>实数可以分为<a href="/wiki/%E6%9C%89%E7%90%86%E6%95%B0" title="有理数">有理数</a>（如<a href="/wiki/42" title="42"><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle 42}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mn>42</mn>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle 42}</annotation>
</semantics>

</p><p>实数可以用来测量<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E8%BF%9E%E7%BB%AD" title="连续">连续</a>變化的量。理论上，任何实数都可以用无限小数的方式表示，小数点的右边是一个无穷的<a href="/wiki/%E6%95%B0%E5%88%97" title="数列">数列</a>（可以是循环的，也可以是非循环的）。在实际运用中，实数经常被近似成一个有限小数（保留小数点后<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle n}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>n</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle n}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="n" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/a601995d55609f2d9f5e233e36fbe9ea26011b3b" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.395ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>位，<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle n}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>n</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle n}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="n" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/a601995d55609f2d9f5e233e36fbe9ea26011b3b" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.395ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>为正整数）。在计算机领域，由于计算机只能存储有限的小数位数，实数经常用<a href="/wiki/%E6%B5%AE%E7%82%B9%E6%95%B0" title="浮点数">浮点数</a>来表示。
</p>
<h2><span id=".E6.AD.A3.E6.95.B0.E4.B8.8E.E8.B4.9F.E6.95.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="正数与负数">正数与负数</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%AE%9E%E6%95%B0&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="编辑章节：正数与负数">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">主条目：<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E6%AD%A3%E6%95%B0" title="正数">正数</a>和<a href="/wiki/%E8%B4%9F%E6%95%B0" title="负数">负数</a></div>
<p>实数是一个<a href="/wiki/%E9%9B%86%E5%90%88_(%E6%95%B0%E5%AD%A6)" title="集合 (数学)">集合</a>，通常可以分为<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E6%AD%A3%E6%95%B0" title="正数">正数</a>、<a href="/wiki/%E8%B4%9F%E6%95%B0" title="负数">负数</a>和<a href="/wiki/0" title="0">零</a>（<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle 0}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mn>0</mn>
</mstyle>
</mrow>

</semantics>

</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle 0}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/2aae8864a3c1fec9585261791a809ddec1489950" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.162ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>與負整數则通常统称为非正整數非常相似。另外，只有实数可以分为正和负等，<a href="/wiki/%E8%99%9A%E6%95%B0" title="虚数">虚数</a>是没有正负之分的。
</p>
<h2><span id=".E5.8E.86.E5.8F.B2"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="历史">历史</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%AE%9E%E6%95%B0&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="编辑章节：历史">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>在公元前500年左右，以<a href="/wiki/%E6%AF%95%E8%BE%BE%E5%93%A5%E6%8B%89%E6%96%AF" title="毕达哥拉斯">毕达哥拉斯</a>为首的<a href="/wiki/%E5%B8%8C%E8%85%8A" title="希腊">希腊</a><a href="/wiki/%E6%95%B0%E5%AD%A6%E5%AE%B6" title="数学家">数学家</a>们認識到有理數在幾何上不能滿足需要，但<a href="/wiki/%E6%AF%95%E8%BE%BE%E5%93%A5%E6%8B%89%E6%96%AF" title="毕达哥拉斯">毕达哥拉斯</a>本身並不承認無理數的存在。
直到17世纪，实数才在欧洲被广泛接受。18世纪，<a href="/wiki/%E5%BE%AE%E7%A7%AF%E5%88%86%E5%AD%A6" title="微积分学">微积分学</a>在实数的基础上发展起来。直到1871年，<a href="/wiki/%E5%BE%B7%E5%9B%BD" title="德国">德国</a><a href="/wiki/%E6%95%B0%E5%AD%A6%E5%AE%B6" title="数学家">数学家</a><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%BA%B7%E6%89%98%E5%B0%94" title="康托尔">康托尔</a>第一次提出了实数的严格定义。
</p>
<h2><span id=".E5.AE.9A.E4.B9.89"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="定义">定义</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%AE%9E%E6%95%B0&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="编辑章节：定义">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span id=".E5.BE.9E.E6.9C.89.E7.90.86.E6.95.B8.E6.9E.84.E9.80.A0.E5.AF.A6.E6.95.B8"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="從有理數构造實數">從有理數构造實數</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%AE%9E%E6%95%B0&amp;action=edit&amp;section=5" title="编辑章节：從有理數构造實數">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>实数可以用通过收敛于一个唯一实数的十进制或二进制展开如<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle {3,3.1,3.14,3.141,3.1415,3.14159...}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mn>3</mn>
<mo>,</mo>
<mn>3.1</mn>
<mo>,</mo>
<mn>3.14</mn>
<mo>,</mo>
<mn>3.141</mn>
<mo>,</mo>
<mn>3.1415</mn>
<mo>,</mo>
<mn>3.14159...</mn>
</mrow>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle {3,3.1,3.14,3.141,3.1415,3.14159...}}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle {3,3.1,3.14,3.141,3.1415,3.14159...}}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/2441e33c4dc9cb3d5c7aeb75cc0f1d534436cc38" style="vertical-align: -0.671ex; width:34.756ex; height:2.509ex;"/></span>所定义的序列的方式而构造为有理数的<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%AE%8C%E5%82%99%E5%8C%96" title="完備化">完備化</a>。實數可以不同方式從<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E6%9C%89%E7%90%86%E6%95%B8" title="有理數">有理數</a>构造出來。这里给出其中一种，其他方法请詳見<a href="/wiki/%E5%AF%A6%E6%95%B8%E7%9A%84%E6%A7%8B%E9%80%A0" title="實數的構造">實數的構造</a>。
</p>
<h3><span id=".E5.85.AC.E7.90.86.E5.8C.96.E6.96.B9.E6.B3.95"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="公理化方法">公理化方法</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%AE%9E%E6%95%B0&amp;action=edit&amp;section=6" title="编辑章节：公理化方法">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>设 <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \mathbb {R} }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

</p>

<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \mathbb {R} }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\R" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/786849c765da7a84dbc3cce43e96aad58a5868dc" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.678ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span> 内有<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E4%B8%8A%E7%A1%AE%E7%95%8C" title="上确界">上确界</a>。</li></ul>
<p>最后一条是区分实数和有理数的关键。例如所有<a href="/wiki/%E5%B9%B3%E6%96%B9" title="平方">平方</a>小于<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle 2}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mn>2</mn>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle 2}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="2" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/901fc910c19990d0dbaaefe4726ceb1a4e217a0f" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.162ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>的有理数的集合存在有理数上界，如<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle 1.5}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mn>1.5</mn>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle 1.5}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle 1.5}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/de4cf334519dcf06a7941d7bb9411c202f77c4ba" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:2.972ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>；但是不存在有理数上确界（因为<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle {\sqrt {2}}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<msqrt>
<mn>2</mn>
</msqrt>
</mrow>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle {\sqrt {2}}}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\sqrt {2}}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/b4afc1e27d418021bf10898eb44a7f5f315735ff" style="vertical-align: -0.671ex; width:3.098ex; height:3.009ex;"/></span>不是有理数）。
</p><p>實數通过上述性质唯一确定。更准确的说，给定任意两个戴德金完备的有序域 <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \mathbb {R} _{1}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<msub>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mi mathvariant="double-struck">R</mi>
</mrow>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mn>1</mn>
</mrow>
</msub>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \mathbb {R} _{1}}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle \mathbb {R} _{1}}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/880c089509beeddaae996a6985f29fb00a7f45e7" style="vertical-align: -0.671ex; width:2.732ex; height:2.509ex;"/></span>和 <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \mathbb {R} _{2}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<msub>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">

</mrow>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">

</mrow>
</msub>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \mathbb {R} _{2}}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle \mathbb {R} _{2}}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/139c792da4e0dfb9cca58316eb540fb919dce79d" style="vertical-align: -0.671ex; width:2.732ex; height:2.509ex;"/></span>，存在从 <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \mathbb {R} _{1}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

</p>
<h2><span id=".E4.BE.8B.E5.AD.90"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="例子">例子</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%AE%9E%E6%95%B0&amp;action=edit&amp;section=7" title="编辑章节：例子">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<ul><li><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle 15}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

<h2><span id=".E6.80.A7.E8.B4.A8"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="性质">性质</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%AE%9E%E6%95%B0&amp;action=edit&amp;section=8" title="编辑章节：性质">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span id=".E5.9F.BA.E6.9C.AC.E8.BF.90.E7.AE.97"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="基本运算">基本运算</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%AE%9E%E6%95%B0&amp;action=edit&amp;section=9" title="编辑章节：基本运算">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>在实数域内，可实现的基本<a href="/wiki/%E8%BF%90%E7%AE%97" title="运算">运算</a>有<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%8A%A0" title="加">加</a>、<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%87%8F" title="减">减</a>、<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E4%B9%98" title="乘">乘</a>、<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E9%99%A4" title="除">除</a>、<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E4%B9%98%E6%96%B9" title="乘方">乘方</a>等，对非负数还可以进行<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E9%96%8B%E6%96%B9" title="開方">开方</a>运算。实数加、减、乘、除（除数不为零）、平方后结果还是实数。任何实数都可以开奇次方，结果仍是实数；只有非负实数才能开偶次方，其结果还是实数。
</p>
<h3><span id=".E8.BF.9E.E7.BB.AD.E6.80.A7.E6.88.96.E5.AE.8C.E5.82.99.E6.80.A7"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="连续性或完備性">连续性或完備性</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%AE%9E%E6%95%B0&amp;action=edit&amp;section=10" title="编辑章节：连续性或完備性">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>作为<a href="/wiki/%E5%BA%A6%E9%87%8F%E7%A9%BA%E9%97%B4" title="度量空间">度量空間</a>或<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E4%B8%80%E8%87%B4%E7%A9%BA%E9%96%93" title="一致空間">一致空間</a>，實數集合是一个<a href="/wiki/%E5%AE%8C%E5%A4%87%E7%A9%BA%E9%97%B4" title="完备空间">完备空间</a>，它有以下性质：
</p>
<dl><dd>所有實數的<a href="/wiki/%E6%9F%AF%E8%A5%BF%E5%BA%8F%E5%88%97" title="柯西序列">柯西序列</a>都有一個實數<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E6%9E%81%E9%99%90_(%E5%BA%8F%E5%88%97)" title="极限 (序列)">極限</a>。</dd></dl>
<p>有理數集合就不是完备空间。例如，<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle (1,1.4,1.41,1.414,1.4142,1.41421,\ldots )}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mo stretchy="false">(</mo>
<mn>1</mn>
<mo>,</mo>
<mn>1.4</mn>
<mo>,</mo>
<mn>1.41</mn>
<mo>,</mo>
<mn>1.414</mn>
<mo>,</mo>
<mn>1.4142</mn>
<mo>,</mo>
<mn>1.41421</mn>
<mo>,</mo>
<mo>…<!-- … --></mo>
<mo stretchy="false">)</mo>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle (1,1.4,1.41,1.414,1.4142,1.41421,\ldots )}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle (1,1.4,1.41,1.414,1.4142,1.41421,\ldots )}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/9f5a6b9c901d3d4f7c77a8c3046b982be3d80d4c" style="vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:38.382ex; height:2.843ex;"/></span>是有理數的柯西序列，但沒有有理數極限。实际上，它有個實數極限<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle {\sqrt {2}}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<msqrt>
<mn>2</mn>
</msqrt>
</mrow>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle {\sqrt {2}}}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\sqrt {2}}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/b4afc1e27d418021bf10898eb44a7f5f315735ff" style="vertical-align: -0.671ex; width:3.098ex; height:3.009ex;"/></span>。實數是有理數的<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%AE%8C%E5%82%99%E5%8C%96" title="完備化">完备化</a>：這亦是构造實數集合的一种方法。
</p>
<h3><span id=".E5.AE.8C.E5.A4.87.E7.9A.84.E6.9C.89.E5.BA.8F.E5.9F.9F.EF.BC.88.E6.9C.89.E5.BA.8F.E6.80.A7.EF.BC.89"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="完备的有序域（有序性）">完备的有序域（有序性）</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%AE%9E%E6%95%B0&amp;action=edit&amp;section=11" title="编辑章节：完备的有序域（有序性）">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>实数集合通常被描述为“完备的有序域”，这可以几种解释。
</p>
<ul><li>首先，有序域可以是<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%AE%8C%E5%A4%87%E6%A0%BC" title="完备格">完备格</a>。然而，很容易发现没有有序域会是完备格。这是由于有序域没有最大元素（对任意元素<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle z}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>z</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle z}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="z" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/bf368e72c009decd9b6686ee84a375632e11de98" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.088ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>，<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle z+1}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>z</mi>
<mo>+</mo>
<mn>1</mn>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle z+1}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle z+1}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/5bd946396897f1d63172e5a7d20c83ec160071e3" style="vertical-align: -0.505ex; width:5.091ex; height:2.343ex;"/></span>将更大）。所以，这裡的“完备”不是完备格的意思。</li>
<li>另外，有序域满足<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E6%88%B4%E5%BE%B7%E9%87%91%E5%AE%8C%E5%A4%87%E6%80%A7" title="戴德金完备性">戴德金完备性</a>，这在上述「公理」中已经定义。上述的唯一性也说明了这裡的“完备”是指戴德金完备性的意思。这个完备性的意思非常接近采用<a href="/wiki/%E6%88%B4%E5%BE%B7%E9%87%91%E5%88%86%E5%89%B2" title="戴德金分割">戴德金分割</a>来构造实数的方法，即从（有理数）有序域出发，通过标准的方法建立戴德金完备性。</li>
<li>这两个完备性的概念都忽略了域的结构。然而，有序<a href="/wiki/%E7%BE%A4" title="群">群</a>（域是种特殊的群）可以定义一致空间，而一致空间又有<a href="/wiki/%E5%AE%8C%E5%A4%87%E7%A9%BA%E9%97%B4" title="完备空间">完备空间</a>的概念。上述「完备性」中所述的只是一个特例。（这里采用一致空间中的完备性概念，而不是相关的人们熟知的度量空间的完备性，这是由于度量空间的定义依赖于实数的性质。）当然，<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \mathbb {R} }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mi mathvariant="double-struck">R</mi>
</mrow>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \mathbb {R} }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\R" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/786849c765da7a84dbc3cce43e96aad58a5868dc" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.678ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>并不是<i>唯一的</i>一致完备的有序域，但它是唯一的一致完备的「<a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E9%98%BF%E5%9F%BA%E7%B1%B3%E5%BE%B7%E5%9F%9F&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="阿基米德域（页面不存在）">阿基米德域</a>」。实际上，“完备的阿基米德域”比“完备的有序域”更常见。可以证明，任意一致完备的阿基米德域必然是戴德金完备的（当然反之亦然）。这个完备性的意思非常接近采用柯西序列来构造实数的方法，即从（有理数）阿基米德域出发，通过标准的方法建立一致完备性。</li>
<li>“完备的阿基米德域”最早是由<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%B8%8C%E5%B0%94%E4%BC%AF%E7%89%B9" title="希尔伯特">希尔伯特</a>提出来的，他还想表达一些不同于上述的意思。他认为，实数构成了「最大的」阿基米德域，即所有其他的阿基米德域都是<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \mathbb {R} }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mi mathvariant="double-struck">R</mi>
</mrow>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \mathbb {R} }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\R" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/786849c765da7a84dbc3cce43e96aad58a5868dc" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.678ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>的子域。这样<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \mathbb {R} }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mi mathvariant="double-struck">R</mi>
</mrow>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \mathbb {R} }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\R" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/786849c765da7a84dbc3cce43e96aad58a5868dc" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.678ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>是“完备的”是指，在其中加入任何元素都将使它不再是阿基米德域。这个完备性的意思非常接近用<a href="/wiki/%E8%B6%85%E5%AE%9E%E6%95%B0_(%E9%9D%9E%E6%A0%87%E5%87%86%E5%88%86%E6%9E%90)" title="超实数 (非标准分析)">超实数</a>来构造实数的方法，即从某个包含所有（超实数）有序域的纯类出发，从其子域中找出最大的阿基米德域。</li></ul>
<h3><span id=".E9.AB.98.E7.BA.A7.E6.80.A7.E8.B4.A8"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="高级性质">高级性质</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%AE%9E%E6%95%B0&amp;action=edit&amp;section=12" title="编辑章节：高级性质">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul><li>实数集是<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E4%B8%8D%E5%8F%AF%E6%95%B8" title="不可數">不可数</a>的，也就是说，实数的个数严格多于<a href="/wiki/%E8%87%AA%E7%84%B6%E6%95%B0" title="自然数">自然数</a>的个数（尽管两者都是<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E6%97%A0%E7%A9%B7%E5%A4%A7" title="无穷大">无穷大</a>）。这一点，可以通过<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%BA%B7%E6%89%98%E7%88%BE%E5%B0%8D%E8%A7%92%E7%B7%9A%E6%96%B9%E6%B3%95" title="康托爾對角線方法">康托尔对角线方法</a>证明。实际上，实数集的<a href="/wiki/%E5%8A%BF_(%E6%95%B0%E5%AD%A6)" title="势 (数学)">势</a>为2<sup><i>ω</i></sup>（请参见<a href="/wiki/%E8%BF%9E%E7%BB%AD%E7%BB%9F%E7%9A%84%E5%8A%BF" title="连续统的势">连续统的势</a>），即<a href="/wiki/%E8%87%AA%E7%84%B6%E6%95%B0" title="自然数">自然数</a>集的<a href="/wiki/%E5%86%AA%E9%9B%86" title="冪集">幂集</a>的势。由于实数集中只有<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%8F%AF%E6%95%B0%E9%9B%86" title="可数集">可数集</a>个数的元素可能是<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E4%BB%A3%E6%95%B0%E6%95%B0" title="代数数">代数数</a>，<a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E7%BB%9D%E5%A4%A7%E5%A4%9A%E6%95%B0&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="绝大多数（页面不存在）">绝大多数</a>实数是<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E8%B6%85%E8%B6%8A%E6%95%B0" title="超越数">超越数</a>。实数集的子集中，不存在其势严格大于自然数集的势且严格小于实数集的势的集合，这就是<a href="/wiki/%E8%BF%9E%E7%BB%AD%E7%BB%9F%E5%81%87%E8%AE%BE" title="连续统假设">连续统假设</a>。该假设不能被证明是否正确，这是因为它和<a href="/wiki/%E9%9B%86%E5%90%88%E8%AE%BA" title="集合论">集合论</a>的<a href="/wiki/%E7%AD%96%E6%A2%85%E6%B4%9B-%E5%BC%97%E5%85%B0%E5%85%8B%E5%B0%94%E9%9B%86%E5%90%88%E8%AE%BA" title="策梅洛-弗兰克尔集合论">ZF(ZFC)公理系统</a>相互独立。</li>
<li>所有非负实数的<a href="/wiki/%E5%B9%B3%E6%96%B9%E6%A0%B9" title="平方根">平方根</a>属于<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle R}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>R</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle R}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="R" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/4b0bfb3769bf24d80e15374dc37b0441e2616e33" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.764ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>，但这对负数不成立。这表明<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle R}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>R</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle R}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="R" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/4b0bfb3769bf24d80e15374dc37b0441e2616e33" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.764ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>上的序是由其代数结构确定的。而且，所有奇数次多项式至少有一个根属于<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle R}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>R</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle R}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="R" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/4b0bfb3769bf24d80e15374dc37b0441e2616e33" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.764ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>。这两个性质使<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle R}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>R</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle R}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="R" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/4b0bfb3769bf24d80e15374dc37b0441e2616e33" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.764ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>成为<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%AF%A6%E5%B0%81%E9%96%89%E5%9F%9F" title="實封閉域">实封闭域</a>的最主要的实例。证明这一点就是对<a href="/wiki/%E4%BB%A3%E6%95%B0%E5%9F%BA%E6%9C%AC%E5%AE%9A%E7%90%86" title="代数基本定理">代数基本定理</a>的证明的前半部分。</li>
<li>实数集拥有一个规范的<a href="/wiki/%E6%B5%8B%E5%BA%A6" title="测度">测度</a>，即<a href="/wiki/%E5%8B%92%E8%B4%9D%E6%A0%BC%E6%B5%8B%E5%BA%A6" title="勒贝格测度">勒贝格测度</a>。</li>
<li>实数集的上确界公理用到了实数集的子集，这是一种二阶逻辑的陈述。不可能只采用<a href="/wiki/%E4%B8%80%E9%98%B6%E9%80%BB%E8%BE%91" title="一阶逻辑">一阶逻辑</a>来刻画实数集：1. <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/L%C3%B6wenheim-Skolem%E5%AE%9A%E7%90%86" title="Löwenheim-Skolem定理">Löwenheim-Skolem定理</a>说明，存在一个实数集的可数稠密子集，它在一阶逻辑中正好满足和实数集自身完全相同的命题；2. <a href="/wiki/%E8%B6%85%E5%AE%9E%E6%95%B0_(%E9%9D%9E%E6%A0%87%E5%87%86%E5%88%86%E6%9E%90)" title="超实数 (非标准分析)">超实数</a>的集合远远大于<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle R}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>R</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle R}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="R" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/4b0bfb3769bf24d80e15374dc37b0441e2616e33" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.764ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>，但也同样满足和<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle R}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">

<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>R</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle R}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="R" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/4b0bfb3769bf24d80e15374dc37b0441e2616e33" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.764ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>的<a href="/wiki/%E9%9D%9E%E6%A0%87%E5%87%86%E6%A8%A1%E5%9E%8B" title="非标准模型">非标准模型</a>。这就是<a href="/wiki/%E9%9D%9E%E6%A0%87%E5%87%86%E5%88%86%E6%9E%90" title="非标准分析">非标准分析</a>的研究内容，在非标准模型中证明一阶逻辑命题（可能比在<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle R}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

<h3><span id=".E6.8B.93.E6.92.B2.E6.80.A7.E8.B3.AA"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="拓撲性質">拓撲性質</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%AE%9E%E6%95%B0&amp;action=edit&amp;section=13" title="编辑章节：拓撲性質">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>實數集構成一個<a href="/wiki/%E5%BA%A6%E9%87%8F%E7%A9%BA%E9%97%B4" title="度量空间">度量空間</a>：<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle x}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>x</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle x}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="x" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/87f9e315fd7e2ba406057a97300593c4802b53e4" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.33ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>和<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle y}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>y</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle y}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="y" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/b8a6208ec717213d4317e666f1ae872e00620a0d" style="vertical-align: -0.671ex; width:1.155ex; height:2.009ex;"/></span>間的距離定為<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E7%B5%95%E5%B0%8D%E5%80%BC" title="絕對值">絕對值</a> <span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle |x-y|}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">

</mrow>
<mi>x</mi>
<mo>−<!-- − --></mo>
<mi>y</mi>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mo stretchy="false">|</mo>
</mrow>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle |x-y|}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle |x-y|}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/9eca622011e2b10520e69a7fa83f3bd75159ab66" style="vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:6.619ex; height:2.843ex;"/></span>。作為一個<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%85%A8%E5%BA%8F%E9%9B%86" title="全序集">全序集</a>，它也具有<a href="/wiki/%E5%BA%8F%E6%8B%93%E6%92%B2" title="序拓撲">序拓撲</a>。這裡，從度量和序關係得到的拓撲相同。實數集又是一<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E7%B6%AD" title="維">維</a>的<a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%8F%AF%E7%B8%AE%E7%A9%BA%E9%96%93&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="可縮空間（页面不存在）">可縮空間</a>（所以也是<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E9%80%A3%E9%80%9A%E7%A9%BA%E9%96%93" title="連通空間">連通空間</a>）、<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%B1%80%E9%83%A8%E7%B4%A7%E8%87%B4%E7%A9%BA%E9%97%B4" title="局部紧致空间">局部緊緻空間</a>、<a href="/wiki/%E5%8F%AF%E5%88%86%E7%A9%BA%E9%97%B4" title="可分空间">可分空間</a>、<span class="ilh-all" data-foreign-title="Baire space" data-lang-code="en" data-lang-name="英语" data-orig-title="貝爾空間"><span class="ilh-page"><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E8%B2%9D%E7%88%BE%E7%A9%BA%E9%96%93&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="貝爾空間（页面不存在）">貝爾空間</a></span><span class="noprint ilh-comment">（<span class="ilh-lang">英语</span><span class="ilh-colon">：</span><span class="ilh-link"><a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Baire_space" title="en:Baire space"><span dir="auto" lang="en">Baire space</span></a></span>）</span></span>。但實數集不是<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E7%B4%A7%E8%87%B4%E7%A9%BA%E9%97%B4" title="紧致空间">緊緻空間</a>。這些可以通過特定的性質來確定，例如，無限連續可分的<a href="/wiki/%E5%BA%8F%E6%8B%93%E6%92%B2" title="序拓撲">序拓撲</a>必須和實數集<a href="/wiki/%E5%90%8C%E8%83%9A" title="同胚">同胚</a>。以下是實數的拓撲性質總覽：
</p>
<ul><li>令<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle a\;}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">

</semantics>

<semantics>

<mspace width="thickmathspace"></mspace>
</mstyle>
</mrow>

</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="a\;" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/ac43f811d675e91eb98db33b8d59ed11866220a1" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.875ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>的<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E9%84%B0%E5%9F%9F" title="鄰域">鄰域</a>是實數集中一個包括一段含有<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle a\;}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

</semantics>

<li><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \mathbb {R} }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

<li><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \mathbb {Q} }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

<li><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \mathbb {R} }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

<li>每個<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \mathbb {R} }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

<li><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \mathbb {R} }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

<li><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \mathbb {R} }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

<li>區間套定理：設<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle (F_{n})_{n\in \mathbb {N} }}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">

</mrow>
</mrow>
</msub>
</mstyle>

<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle (F_{n})_{n\in \mathbb {N} }}</annotation>

<dl><dd><dl><dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \forall n\in \mathbb {N} \;\forall m&gt;n\quad F_{m}\subset F_{n}\quad \Rightarrow \quad \bigcap _{n\in \mathbb {N} }F_{n}\;\neq \varnothing \;}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \forall n\in \mathbb {N} \;\forall m&gt;n\quad F_{m}\subset F_{n}\quad \Rightarrow \quad \bigcap _{n\in \mathbb {N} }F_{n}\;\neq \varnothing \;}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\forall n\in {\mathbb  N}\;\forall m&gt;n\quad F_{m}\subset F_{n}\quad \Rightarrow \quad \bigcap _{{n\in {\mathbb  N}}}F_{n}\;\neq \varnothing \;" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/b663e65999ae96842327f07d675f7e07b70aba78" style="vertical-align: -3.171ex; width:47.806ex; height:5.676ex;"/></span>.</dd></dl></dd></dl>
<h2><span id=".E6.89.A9.E5.B1.95.E4.B8.8E.E4.B8.80.E8.88.AC.E5.8C.96"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="扩展与一般化">扩展与一般化</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%AE%9E%E6%95%B0&amp;action=edit&amp;section=14" title="编辑章节：扩展与一般化">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>实数集可以在几种不同的方面进行扩展和一般化：
</p>
<ul><li>最自然的扩展可能就是<a href="/wiki/%E5%A4%8D%E6%95%B0_(%E6%95%B0%E5%AD%A6)" title="复数 (数学)">复数</a>了。复数集是包含了所有<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%A4%9A%E9%A1%B9%E5%BC%8F" title="多项式">多项式</a>的根的<a href="/wiki/%E4%BB%A3%E6%95%B8%E9%96%89%E5%9F%9F" title="代數閉域">代数闭域</a>。但是，复数集不是一个<a href="/wiki/%E6%9C%89%E5%BA%8F%E5%9F%9F" title="有序域">有序域</a>。</li></ul>
<ul><li>实数集扩展的有序域是<a href="/wiki/%E8%B6%85%E5%AE%9E%E6%95%B0_(%E9%9D%9E%E6%A0%87%E5%87%86%E5%88%86%E6%9E%90)" title="超实数 (非标准分析)">超实数</a>的集合，包含<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E6%97%A0%E7%A9%B7%E5%B0%8F" title="无穷小">无穷小</a>和<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E6%97%A0%E7%A9%B7%E5%A4%A7" title="无穷大">无穷大</a>。它不是一个<a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E9%98%BF%E5%9F%BA%E7%B1%B3%E5%BE%B7%E5%9F%9F&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="阿基米德域（页面不存在）">阿基米德域</a>。</li></ul>
<ul><li>有时候，形式元素 +∞和 -∞加入实数集，构成<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E6%89%A9%E5%B1%95%E7%9A%84%E5%AE%9E%E6%95%B0%E8%BD%B4" title="扩展的实数轴">扩展的实数轴</a>。它是一个紧致空间，而不是一个域，但它保留了许多实数的性质。</li></ul>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/%E5%B8%8C%E5%B0%94%E4%BC%AF%E7%89%B9%E7%A9%BA%E9%97%B4" title="希尔伯特空间">希尔伯特空间</a>的<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E8%87%AA%E4%BC%B4%E9%9A%8F%E7%AE%97%E5%AD%90" title="自伴随算子">自伴随算子</a>在许多方面一般化实数集：它们可以是有序的（尽管不一定全序）、完备的；它们所有的<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E7%89%B9%E5%BE%81%E5%80%BC" title="特征值">特征值</a>都是实数；它们构成一个实<a href="/wiki/%E7%B5%90%E5%90%88%E4%BB%A3%E6%95%B8" title="結合代數">结合代数</a>。</li></ul>
<h2><span id=".E6.B3.A8.E9.87.8A"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="注释">注释</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%AE%9E%E6%95%B0&amp;action=edit&amp;section=15" title="编辑章节：注释">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>

<ol class="references">
<li id="cite_note-1"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-1">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">《数学辞海（第一卷）》山西教育出版社 中国科学技术出版社 东南大学出版社</span>
</li>
</ol></div>
<h2><span id=".E8.AF.B7.E5.8F.82.E9.98.85"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="请参阅">请参阅</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%AE%9E%E6%95%B0&amp;action=edit&amp;section=16" title="编辑章节：请参阅">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
